 isse pehle, congress va upie adhyaksh sonia gandhi ke bulaave par dilli pahunchin pashchim bengal kii mukhyamantri va trinmul congress kii pramukh mamata banerjee kii sonia se hui mulaakaat se pehle sutron ne jaankaree di thi ki mamata kii list main pranab mukherjee kaa naam sabase neeche he, jabaki unki pasand ke taur par pashchim bengal ke purv rajyapal gopal gandhi, loksabhaa adhyaksh mira kumaar or purv raashtrapati apije abdul kalam ke naam sutron ne bataae the
 However, meeting Mamata's Samajwadi Party chief Mulayam Singh Yadav on Tuesday before meeting Sonia was seen as a murmur of new equations and it was believed that Mamata had asked Finance Minister Pranab Mukherjee for upa's candidature for the presidency
 Has agreed in the name of
 unhone kaha bhi tha ki is baat se unhen khushi hogi, yadi desh ke is sarvocch pad par bengal kaa koi netaa aae
 But he also wishes that the Congress opens its cards first, and declares Pranab's name as a candidate
 tippaniyan On the other hand, the Congress has given the right to choose the candidate on its behalf to Sonia Gandhi, but she is also aware that the Congress does not have enough votes to give its candidate a definite victory, hence Mulayam Singh's SP and Mamta That Trinamool's support will be compulsory for the Congress, and perhaps that's why Sonia Gandhi wants to be fully satisfied before announcing the candidate on her behalf
 philhal congress kaa daawa he ki is maamle main puraa upie ek he, or unke is daawey ko is baat se bhi bal miltaa he ki mayawati kii bispi, or karunanidhi kii diemke bhi pranab ke naam par sahmati jataa chuke hai
 It is also being said that the Congress wants to settle this issue by Friday, June 15, and that is why Pranab has canceled his visit to Kabul starting on the 14th, which has led to speculation again
 is mudde main yah jaankaree bhi ahm he ki pradhanmantri dow manmohan singh 16 june se brazil va mexico kii yatra par ja rahe hai, or jald hi upie adhyaksh bhi ilaaj ke liye videsh jane vaali hai
 Meanwhile, the Nationalist Congress Party (NCP) has also made such a statement, which is going right in the direction of Pranab, so all the gestures are saying that Pranab is in the forefront of becoming the new highness of the country
 But the only problem is that the Congress has not officially named him yet
 raashtrapati pad ke pratyaashee ke liye mulaayam singh yadav or mamata banerjee ne buudhvaar ko teen naamon par charchaa kii he
 Both leaders say that if a consensus is reached on these three names, it would be welcome
 vahiin, is khabar ke baad ensipi netaa sharad pavaar ne kaha ki ab yah jaruri he ki sabhi partiyon se ek baar phir baatcheet kii jaae
 On the statement of Mamta and Mulayam, he says that it is not right for him to say anything on any one name
 sapa or trinmul congress kii ore se raashtrapati pad ke liye sujhaaye gaye teen naamon par bhaajapa ne aaj charchaa kii lekin kaha ki congress dwaara is sheersh sanvaidhanik pad ke ummidavaar kii ghoshnaa kiye jane ke baad hi vah apni pratikriya degi
 Meanwhile, PMO office minister Narayanasamy went to meet the finance minister and details of the talks have not been received
 congress party ne der shaam yah ghoshnaa kii ki unki pasand kaa hi ummidavaar raashtrapati chunaav main jeet hasil karegaa
 Sources are also telling that after the Prime Minister returns from abroad, the matter will be discussed and the final decision for the name of the President will also be taken when the PM comes home
 gauratlab he ki kuch ghanton pehle hi mamata banerjee ne sonia gandhi se mulaakaat karne ke baad kaha ki apni party trinmul ke netaaon se salaah lekar vah koi antim faisla lengi
 However, Mamata made it clear that Pranab Mukherjee is the first choice of Congress President Sonia Gandhi as the presidential candidate, while she wants to see the current Vice President Hamid Ansari as the second choice
 is mulaakaat ke baad mamata banerjee sidhe mulaayam singh yadav ke ghar gayi or kaha ja rahaa he ki vahaan par bhi mamata banerjee raashtrapati pad ke ummidavaar ke bare main charchaa karengi
 Earlier, before the meeting of West Bengal Chief Minister and Trinamool Congress chief Mamata Banerjee reached Delhi on the call of Congress and UPA President Sonia Gandhi, sources had informed that Pranab Mukherjee's name is at the bottom of Mamta's list, While his choice was former West Bengal Governor Gopal Gandhi, Lok Sabha Speaker Meira Kumar and former President APJ a Dul Kalam sources were telling him
 haalanki sonia se mulaakaat se pehle mangalvaar ko mamata kii samaajawaadee party pramukh mulaayam singh yadav se milanaa nae sameekaran kii sugabugahat ke taur par dekha ja rahaa tha or mana ja rahaa tha ki mamata ne raashtrapati pad kii upie kii ore se ummidavaari ke liye vittamantri pranab mukherjee ke naam par sahmati de di he
 He had also said that he would be happy with this, if a leader of Bengal comes to this highest post of the country
 parantu unki yah bhi ichha he ki congress pehle apane pattey khole, or ummidavaar ke rup main pranab ke naam kaa elaan kare
 The comments duusari ore, congress apni ore se ummidavaar chunane kaa adhikaar sonia gandhi ko de chuki he, lekin unhen yah bhi dhyaan he ki congress ke paas apane itane vot nahin hai ki ve apane ummidavaar ko nishchit jeet dilaa saken, isliye mulaayam singh kii sapa or mamata kii trinmul kaa saath congress ke liye anivaary hoga, or shaayad isiilie sonia gandhi apni ore se ummidavaar kaa elaan karne se pehle puri tasalli kar lenaa chaahati hai
 At present, the Congress claims that the entire UPA is one in this case, and their claim is also bolstered by the fact that Mayawati's BSP, and Karunanidhi's DMK have also agreed on Pranab's name
 yah bhi kaha ja rahaa he ki congress shuukravaar, 15 june tak yah masalaa nipta lenaa chaahati he, or isiilie pranab ne 14 taarikh se shuru hone vaala apana kabul daura radd kar diya he, jisase phir atakalein lagane lagi hai
 It is also important to know in this issue that Prime Minister Dr
 Manmohan Singh is going to visit Brazil and Mexico from 16 June, and soon the UPA President will also be going abroad for treatment
 is bich, rashtravaadi congress party (ensipi) ne bhi aisa bayaan diya he, jo ishaaron main hi sahi, pranab ke haq main ja rahaa he, so, saare ishaare yahi bataa rahe hai ki pranab desh ke nae mahamahim banane kii daud main sabase aage hai, lekin mushkil sirf itani he ki congress ne abhi aadhikarik taur par unka naam nahin liya he
 At the same time, after this news NCP leader Sharad Pawar said that now it is necessary that all the parties once again have a dialogue
 mamata or mulaayam ke bayaan par unka kahana he ki kisi ek naam par unka kuch kahana philhal thik nahin he
 The BJP today discussed the three names suggested by the SP and Trinamool Congress for the presidency but said it would react only after the Congress announced the top constitutional nominee
 udhar der shaam piemo karyaalay ke mantri narayansami vittamantri se milane gaye or baatcheet kaa byoraa hasil nahin ho paaya he
 The Congress party announced late in the evening that the candidate of their choice would win the presidential election
 sutara yah bhi bataa rahe hai pradhanmantri ke videsh se lautne ke baad is maamle par charchaa kii jaaegi or raashtrapati pad ke liye naam bhi antim faisla piem ke swadesh aane par liya jayega
 Significantly, after meeting Sonia Gandhi a few hours ago, Mamata Banerjee said that she would take a final decision after consulting the leaders of her party's Trinamool

 This may be part of a clue in my mind, but I'm not going to speculate on what it actually means
 ' He, however, clarified that India 'is not going to leave any piece of land
 ' rahaa ne bharat or china kii sena ke baar-baar aamane-saamne hone ke liye vaastavik niyantran rekha ke paas donon deshon kii vaastavik sthiti ko lekar alag-alag vichaar hone ko jimmedaar bataaya

 COP-14 main Bamboonomics par bharat ko riprogent karegaa ye khiladisheli shaury ne adivaasiyon kii arthvyavastha ko majubat banane kaa bejod formula diaindian premier lig (ipel) ke gujarat liance team kaa hissaa rahe or manipur kii ore se ranjai trophy khilne vaale shelli shaury ne adivaasiyon kii arthvyavastha ko majboot banane kaa bejod formula diya he
 The Modi government is also implementing his formula
 25 saal ke shelli shaury ne Bamboonomics par jo theory di he, uske jariye bans se acchhee kamai ke saath-saath badhate pradooshan ko bhi niyantrit kiya ja saktaa he
 196 countries are participating in COP-14
 Actually, Modi government wants to make tribals competent and prosperous by implementing bamboo-based economy
 yahi vajah he ki 2017 main bans ko ped kii shrenee se hataakar ghaas ghoshit kiya gaya
 Considering the growing demand from bamboo, the plan for environmentally friendly Bamboonomics is to be presented today at COP-14 (conference of Parties) by the tribal ministry
 is conference main Bamboonomics par shelli shaury bharat ko riprogent kar rahe hai
 Significantly, COP-14 is organized to save the world from increasing desertification
 duniya ke 196 deshon ke pratinidhi is conference main bhaag le rahe hai
 The goal of making barren land fertile has been increased
 On September 9, Prime Minister Narendra Modi also reached this conference going on from September 2
 is dauraan unhone kaha tha ki bharat 2030 tak 2
 2, increasing its target to make 1 crore hectares of barren land fertile
 6 karod hectare karegaa
 To tackle desertification, Modi said that between 2015 and 2017, the area of trees and forests in India has increased by 8 lakh hectares

 jab bachche is hinsa ko bardaasht nahin kar paaenge to ve mata-pita ke khilaaf police se hastkshep karne ke liye kehane ko swatantra honge

 6 fisadi bacchon ko parivaar main unke mata-pita hi maarthe-peetate hai
